<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приладить.html>прила́дить</a> (19997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приладить.html>прила́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priláditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилаживать.html>прила́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attach, to fasten <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative, to something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fit (clothing)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приладить.html>прила́женный</a> (19997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приладить.html>прила́женный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prilážennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приладить.html>прила́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priláditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***приласкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приласкать.html>приласка́ть</a> (20598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласкать.html>ласка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">laskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приласкать.html>приласка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prilaskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласкать.html>ласка́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to caress <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">touch, kiss or stroke lovingly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to fondle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be nice to someone, to show a friendly disposition</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"><a href = vnd.unilang:будущий.html>бу́дущ</a>.
</th>

***прилегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прилегать.html>прилега́ть</a> (11435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилегать.html>прилега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prilegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to adjoin, to border
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Cад <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прилегать.html>прилега́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реке́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Cad <b>prilegájet</b> k reké</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The garden adjoins the river.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fit snugly on, to fit closely</li>
<li>to cling to</li></ol>

***прилетать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прилетать.html>прилета́ть</a> (11719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилететь.html>прилете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priletétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилетать.html>прилета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилететь.html>прилете́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to land; to touch down</li>
<li>to descend to soil (flying).</li>
<li>(<i>used figuratively</i>) to arrive swiftly, to abruptly (sometimes unexpectedly)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взлетать.html>взлета́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzletátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(antonym)</i></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прилететь.html>прилете́ть</a> (3679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилететь.html>прилете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priletétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилетать.html>прилета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly (here), to arrive (by flying)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прилечь.html>приле́чь</a> (8552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилечь.html>приле́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priléčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to lie down (<i>for a short period</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прилечь.html>приля́гу</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>буди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́ну</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>priljágu</b>, ne budí menjá požálujsta, ja sam vstánu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'll lie down, don't wake me up please, I'll get up myself.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***прилив.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прилив.html>прилив</a> (8624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилив.html>прили́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prilív</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилив.html>прили́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилив.html>прили́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилив.html>прили́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tide</li>
<li>high tide</li>
<li>flood, flow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rush</li>
<li>congestion</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прилипать.html>прилипа́ть</a> (22224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилипнуть.html>прили́пнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prilípnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилипать.html>прилипа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prilipátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилипнуть.html>прили́пнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick, to adhere, to cleave</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:липнуть.html>ли́пнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lípnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прилепля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prilepljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилепить.html>прилепи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prilepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:липнуть.html>ли́пнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lípnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a> (3345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагать.html>прилага́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put (next to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priložítʹ</b> časý k úxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a watch to one's ear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырьку́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priložítʹ</b> rúku k kozyrʹkú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put one's hand to the peak of one's cap, salute</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priložítʹ</b> rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to sign, fix one's signature 2) take a hand (in), put one's hand, to have a finger in the pie</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prikládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to enclose, to join, to attach
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priložítʹ</b> pečátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attach a seal</span></div></dd>

<ol><li>to put oneself <i>(to)</i>, to press oneself <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладываться.html>прикла́дываться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земле́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prikládyvatʹsja úxom k zemlé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put one's ear to the ground</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kiss</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́ма</a> (7214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">prima</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">príma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́м</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tonic, unison interval</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">príma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прима.html>при́м</a></b>)
